style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">靠</SPAN>的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -4.85pt">，</SPAN>企业应<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">当</SPAN>以换入<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产的</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">公允价值<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">为</SPAN>基础确<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">定</SPAN>换入资<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">产</SPAN>的初始<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">计</SPAN>量金额<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -4.85pt">，</SPAN>换<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">入</SPAN>资产的公<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">允</SPAN>价值与<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">换</SPAN>出资产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">账</SPAN>面价值之</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">间的差额<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">计</SPAN>入当期<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">损</SPAN>益<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt">。</SPAN>二是<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">以</SPAN>账面价<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">值</SPAN>为基础<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">计量</SPAN>的非货币<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">性</SPAN>资产交换<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.65pt">，</SPAN>企业应<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">当</SPAN>以换出</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">资产的账<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">面</SPAN>价值为<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">基</SPAN>础确定<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">换</SPAN>入资产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">的</SPAN>初始计<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">量</SPAN>金<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">额</SPAN>，换出资<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">产</SPAN>终止确<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">认</SPAN>时不确<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">认</SPAN>损益。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><A name=（二）商业实质的判断></A><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（二）商业实质的判断<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 3.1pt 10.5pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">根据本准则的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">规</SPAN>定，满足<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">下</SPAN>列条件之<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">一</SPAN>的非货币性<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产交换具有商<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">业</SPAN>实质：（</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">换入</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">资产的未来现<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">金</SPAN>流量在风<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">险</SPAN>、时间分<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">布</SPAN>或金额方<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">面与</SPAN>换出资产显著<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">不</SPAN>同。（</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">）<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">使</SPAN>用换入资</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">产</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">所<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt">产</SPAN>生的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt">预</SPAN>计未<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt">来</SPAN>现<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt">金</SPAN>流量<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt">现</SPAN>值与<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt">继</SPAN>续<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt">使</SPAN>用换<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt">出</SPAN>资<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt">产</SPAN>所<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt">产</SPAN>生的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt">预</SPAN>计未<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt">来</SPAN>现<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt">金</SPAN>流量<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt">现</SPAN>值不</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">同，且其<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">差</SPAN>额与换<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">入</SPAN>资产和<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">换</SPAN>出资产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">的</SPAN>公允价<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">值</SPAN>相<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">比</SPAN>是重大的。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 1.8pt 0cm 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">在判断资<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">产</SPAN>交换是<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">否</SPAN>具有商<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">业</SPAN>实质时<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -4.85pt">，</SPAN>企<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">业</SPAN>应当重<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">点</SPAN>考虑由于<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">发</SPAN>生了该<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">项</SPAN>资产交<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">换</SPAN>预计</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">使企业未<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">来</SPAN>现金流<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">量</SPAN>发生变<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">动</SPAN>的程度<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -4.8pt">。</SPAN>只<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">有</SPAN>当换入<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产的未来<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">现</SPAN>金流量<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">和</SPAN>换出资<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">产</SPAN>的未来现</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">金流量相<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">比</SPAN>发生较<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">大</SPAN>变化<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -4.85pt">，</SPAN>或使<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">用</SPAN>换入资<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">产</SPAN>进行经<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">营</SPAN>和继续使<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">用</SPAN>换出资<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">产</SPAN>进行经<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">营</SPAN>所产生的</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">预计未来<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">现</SPAN>金流量<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">现</SPAN>值之间<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">的</SPAN>差额较<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">大</SPAN>时<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -4.85pt">，</SPAN>才表明<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">该</SPAN>交易的发<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">生</SPAN>使企业<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">经</SPAN>济状况<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">发</SPAN>生了明显</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">改变，交换才<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">因</SPAN>而具有商<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">业</SPAN>实质。企<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">业</SPAN>应当根据<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">本准</SPAN>则的规定，遵<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">循</SPAN>实质重于<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">形</SPAN>式的原则，</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">判断非货<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">币</SPAN>性资产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">交</SPAN>换是否<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">具</SPAN>有商业<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">实</SPAN>质。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt 27.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1.</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">判断条件。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">（</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>1</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">）换入资产的未来现金流量在风险、时间分布或金额方面与换出资产显著不同。</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">企业应当对比考虑换入资产与换出资产的未来现金流量在风险、时间或金额的三个方面，对非货币性资产交换是否具有商业实质进行综合判断。通常情况下，只要换入资产和换出资产的未来现金流量在风险、时间或金额中的某个方面存在显著不同，即表明满足商业实质的判断条件。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 1.8pt 0cm 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">例如，企业以一项生产用的设备换入一批存货，设备作为固定资产要在较长的时间内为</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">企业带来现金流量，而存货流动性强，能够在较短的时间内产生现金流量。两者产生现金流</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">量的时间相差较大，即使假定两者产生未来现金流量的风险和总额均相同，可以认为上述固</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">定资产与存货的未来现金流量显著不同，因而交换具有商业实质。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">又如<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt">，</SPAN>甲企<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">业</SPAN>以其用<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">于</SPAN>经营出<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">租</SPAN>的一幢<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">公</SPAN>寓楼<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt">，</SPAN>与<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">乙</SPAN>企业同样<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">用</SPAN>于经营<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">出</SPAN>租的一<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">幢</SPAN>公寓</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">楼进行交换<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">两</SPAN>幢公寓<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">楼</SPAN>的租期<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">、</SPAN>每<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">期</SPAN>租金总<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">额</SPAN>均<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">相</SPAN>同<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">，</SPAN>但是甲企<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">业</SPAN>的公寓<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">楼</SPAN>是租给<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">一</SPAN>家财</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">务及信用状况<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">良</SPAN>好的知名<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">上</SPAN>市公司作<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">为</SPAN>职工宿舍<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">，乙</SPAN>企业的公寓楼<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">则</SPAN>是租给多<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">个</SPAN>个人租户。</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">相比较而言<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.65pt">，</SPAN>甲企业<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">无</SPAN>法取得<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">租</SPAN>金的风<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">险</SPAN>较小<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt">，</SPAN>乙<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">企</SPAN>业取得租<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">金</SPAN>依赖于<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">各</SPAN>个个人<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">租</SPAN>户的财务</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">和信用状况<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.65pt">，</SPAN>两者现<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">金</SPAN>流量流<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">入</SPAN>的风险<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">或</SPAN>不确定<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">性程</SPAN>度存在明<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">显</SPAN>差异<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt">，</SPAN>可<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">以</SPAN>认为两<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">幢</SPAN>公寓楼</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">的未来现<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">金</SPAN>流量显<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">著</SPAN>不同，<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">因</SPAN>而交换<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">具</SPAN>有商业<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">实</SPAN>质。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">（</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">）使用换入<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产所产生<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">的</SPAN>预计未来<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">现</SPAN>金流量现<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">值</SPAN>与继续使用换<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">出</SPAN>资产所产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">生</SPAN>的预计</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">未来现金<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">流</SPAN>量现值<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">不</SPAN>同，且<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">其</SPAN>差额与<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">换</SPAN>入资产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">和</SPAN>换<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">出</SPAN>资产的公<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">允</SPAN>价值相<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">比</SPAN>是重大<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">的</SPAN>。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 2.3pt 15.5pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">企业如果按照<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">上</SPAN>述第（</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">）<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">项</SPAN>判断条件<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">难</SPAN>以判断非<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">货</SPAN>币性资产交换<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">是</SPAN>否具有商<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">业</SPAN>实质，</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">可以按照第（</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">项条件，<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">分</SPAN>别计算使<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">用</SPAN>换入资产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">进</SPAN>行相关经营的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">预</SPAN>计未来现<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">金</SPAN>流量现值和</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">继续使用<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">换</SPAN>出资产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">进</SPAN>行相关<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">经</SPAN>营的预<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">计</SPAN>未来现<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">金</SPAN>流<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">量</SPAN>现值<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt">，</SPAN>通过<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">二</SPAN>者比较<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">进</SPAN>行判断<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt">。</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">企</SPAN>业在</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">计算预计<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">未</SPAN>来现金<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">流</SPAN>量现值时<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -4.8pt">，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">应</SPAN>当按照<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产在企<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">业</SPAN>自身持续<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">使</SPAN>用过程<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">和</SPAN>最终处<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">置</SPAN>时预计产</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">生的税后<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">未</SPAN>来现金<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">流</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">量</SPAN>（使用企<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">业</SPAN>自身的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">所</SPAN>得税税<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">率</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">），</SPAN>根据企业自身<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">而</SPAN>不是市<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">场</SPAN>参与者对</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">资产特定<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">风</SPAN>险的评价<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.65pt">，</SPAN>选择恰<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">当</SPAN>的折现<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">率</SPAN>对预计<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">未来</SPAN>现金流量<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">折</SPAN>现后的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">金</SPAN>额加以<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">确</SPAN>定<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt">，</SPAN>以体</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">现资产对<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">企</SPAN>业自身<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">的</SPAN>特定价<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">值</SPAN>。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 2.3pt 15.5pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">从市场参与者的角度分析，换入资产和换出资产的未来现金流量在风险、时间或金额方</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">面可能相同或相似。但是对于企业自身而言，鉴于换入资产的性质和换入企业经营活动的特</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">征等因素，换入资产与换入企业其他现有资产相结合，能够比换出资产发挥更大的作用，使换入企业受该换入资产影响的经营活动部分产生的现金流量与换出资产明显不同，进而使用</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">换入资产进行相关经营的预计未来现金流量现值与继续使用换出资产进行相关经营的预计</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">未来现金流量现值存在重大差异，当其差额与换入资产和换出资产的公允价值相比是重大的，</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">则表明交换具有商业实质。例如，甲企业以持有的某非上市公司</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>A</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">企业的</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>10%</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">股权换入乙企</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">业拥有的一项专利权。假定从市场参与者的角度来看，该股权与该项专利权的公允价值相同，</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">两项资产未来现金流量的风险、时间和金额亦相似。通过第（</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>1</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">）项判断条件难以得出交易</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">是否具有商业实质的结论。根据第（</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>2</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">）项判断条件，对换入专利权的甲企业来说，该项专利权能够解决其生产中的技术难题，使其未来的生产产量成倍增长，从而产生的预计未来现</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">金流量现值与换出的股权投资有较大差异，且其差额与换入资产和换出资产的公允价值相比</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">是重大的，因而可认为该交换具有商业实质。对换入股权的乙企业来说，其取得甲公司换出</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">的</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>A</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">企业</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>10%</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">股权后，对</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>A</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">企业的投资关系由重大影响变为控制，从而产生的预计未来现金</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">流量现值与换出的专利权有较大差异，且其差额与换入资产和换出资产的公允价值相比也是</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">重大的，因而可认为该交换具有商业实质。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>2.</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">判断商业实质时对资产类别的考虑。企业在判断非货币性资产交换是否具有商业实质时，通常还可以考虑资产是否属于同一类别来进行分析。同类别的资产是指在资产负债表中列示为同一报表项目的资产；不同类别的资产是指在资产负债表中列示为不同报表项目的资产，例如存货、固定资产、无形资产、投资性房地产、长期股权投资等都是不同类别的非货币性资产。一<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">般</SPAN>来说<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">，</SPAN>不同<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">类</SPAN>别的非货币性资产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">产</SPAN>生经济<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">利</SPAN>益的方<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">式</SPAN>不同<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt">，</SPAN>其<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">产</SPAN>生的未<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">来现</SPAN>金流量在<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">风</SPAN>险<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt">、</SPAN>时间<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">或</SPAN>金额方<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">面</SPAN>也很可能不相同<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">。</SPAN>不<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">同</SPAN>类别非<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">货</SPAN>币性资<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">产</SPAN>之间的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">交</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">换</SPAN>（如<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">存</SPAN>货和固定<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产之间<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">的</SPAN>交换<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">、</SPAN>固定<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产和长期股权<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">投</SPAN>资之间<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">的</SPAN>交换等<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">）</SPAN>是<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">否</SPAN>具有商<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">业</SPAN>实质<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">通</SPAN>常较易判断<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">；</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">而</SPAN>同类别<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">非</SPAN>货币性<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产之间的交换（如<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">存</SPAN>货之间、<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">固</SPAN>定资产之<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">间</SPAN>、长期股<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">权投</SPAN>资之间的交换<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">等</SPAN>）是否具<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">有</SPAN>商业实质，则通常较<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">难</SPAN>判断，<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">需</SPAN>要根据<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">上</SPAN>述两项<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">判</SPAN>断条件<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">综</SPAN>合<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">判</SPAN>断。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 10.5pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">例如<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">，</SPAN>企业将<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">一</SPAN>项用于<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">出</SPAN>租的投<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>性房地产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">与</SPAN>另<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">一</SPAN>企业的厂<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">房</SPAN>进行交换<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">换</SPAN>入的厂房</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">作为自用<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">固</SPAN>定资产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">，</SPAN>属<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">于</SPAN>不同类<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">别</SPAN>的非货<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">币</SPAN>性资产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">之</SPAN>间的交换<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">。</SPAN>在<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">该</SPAN>交换交<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">易</SPAN>下<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">，</SPAN>换出的投</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">资性房地<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">产</SPAN>的未来<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">现</SPAN>金流量<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">为</SPAN>每期的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">租</SPAN>金<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -4.85pt">，</SPAN>换入的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">固</SPAN>定资产的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">未</SPAN>来现金<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">流</SPAN>量为该<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">厂</SPAN>房独立产</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">生<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">、</SPAN>或包括该<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">厂</SPAN>房的资<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">产</SPAN>组协同<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">产</SPAN>生的现<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">金</SPAN>流量<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">。</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">通</SPAN>常情况下<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">，</SPAN>由<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">定</SPAN>期租金<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">带</SPAN>来的现<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">金</SPAN>流量</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">与用于生<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">产</SPAN>经营的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">固</SPAN>定资产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">产</SPAN>生的现<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">金</SPAN>流量在<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">风</SPAN>险<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.65pt">、</SPAN>时间或金<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">额</SPAN>方面显<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">著</SPAN>不同<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt">，</SPAN>因<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">而</SPAN>两项资</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">产的交换<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">具</SPAN>有商业<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">实</SPAN>质。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">再如<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt">，</SPAN>企业<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">将</SPAN>其拥有<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">的</SPAN>一幢建<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">筑</SPAN>物<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt">，</SPAN>与另<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">一</SPAN>企业拥<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">有</SPAN>的在同地<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">点</SPAN>的另一<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">幢</SPAN>建筑物<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">进</SPAN>行交</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">换，两幢建筑<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">物</SPAN>的建造时<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">间</SPAN>、建造成<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">本</SPAN>等均相同<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">，属</SPAN>于同类别的非<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">货</SPAN>币性资产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">之</SPAN>间的交换。</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">在该交换<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">交</SPAN>易下<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.25pt">，</SPAN>两<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">幢</SPAN>建筑物<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">未</SPAN>来现<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">金</SPAN>流量的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">风</SPAN>险<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.45pt">、</SPAN>时间和金<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">额</SPAN>可能相同<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.45pt">，</SPAN>也可能<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">不</SPAN>同<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.25pt">。</SPAN>如</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">果其中一<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">幢</SPAN>建筑物<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">可</SPAN>以立即<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">出</SPAN>售<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt">，</SPAN>企业<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">管</SPAN>理层也<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">打算</SPAN>将其立即<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">出</SPAN>售<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt">，</SPAN>而另<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">一</SPAN>幢建筑<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">物</SPAN>难以出</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">售或只能<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">在</SPAN>一段较<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">长</SPAN>的时间<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">内</SPAN>出售<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt">，</SPAN>则<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">可</SPAN>以表明<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">两项</SPAN>资产未来<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">现</SPAN>金流量<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">的</SPAN>风险<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt">、</SPAN>时<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">间</SPAN>或金额</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">显著不同<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">，</SPAN>因而这<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">两</SPAN>项资产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">的</SPAN>交换具<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">有</SPAN>商业实<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">质</SPAN>。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 10.5pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">此外<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt">，</SPAN>需要<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">说</SPAN>明的是<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt">，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">从</SPAN>事相同<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">经</SPAN>营业务<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">的</SPAN>企业之<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">间</SPAN>相互交换<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">具</SPAN>有类似<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">性</SPAN>质和相<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">等</SPAN>价值</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">的商品<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">，</SPAN>以便<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">在</SPAN>不同地<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">区</SPAN>销售<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">，</SPAN>这种<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">同</SPAN>类别的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">非</SPAN>货<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">币</SPAN>性资产之<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">间</SPAN>的交换<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">不</SPAN>具有商<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">业</SPAN>实质<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">。</SPAN>实</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">务中，这<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">种</SPAN>交换通<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">常</SPAN>发生在<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">某</SPAN>些特定<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">商</SPAN>品上，<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">常</SPAN>见<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">的</SPAN>例子如石<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">油</SPAN>或牛奶<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">等</SPAN>。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><A name=六、关于以公允价值为基础计量></A><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>六、关于以公允价值为基础计量<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 4.05pt 10.5pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">根据本准<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">则</SPAN>的规定<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt">，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">非</SPAN>货币性<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产交换<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">具</SPAN>有商业<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">实质</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt">，</SPAN>且换入资<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">产</SPAN>或换出<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产的公<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">允</SPAN>价</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">值能够可<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">靠</SPAN>地计量的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">企</SPAN>业应当<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">以</SPAN>公允价<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">值</SPAN>为基础<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">计</SPAN>量<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">。</SPAN>实务中<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">，</SPAN>企业<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">在</SPAN>进行非<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">货</SPAN>币性资产交换时<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -5.05pt">，</SPAN>相<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">关</SPAN>换入资<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">产</SPAN>或换出<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产的公<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">允</SPAN>价值通<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">常会</SPAN>在合同中<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">约</SPAN>定<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -5.05pt">；</SPAN>对于<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">合</SPAN>同中没<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">有</SPAN>约定的，</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">应当按照<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">合</SPAN>同开始<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">日</SPAN>（合同<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">生</SPAN>效日）<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">的</SPAN>公允价<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">值</SPAN>确<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">定</SPAN>。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 1.65pt 10.5pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">本准则规定<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.65pt">，</SPAN>换入资<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">产</SPAN>和换出<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产的公<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">允</SPAN>价值均<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">能够</SPAN>可靠计量的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.65pt">，</SPAN>应当以<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">换</SPAN>出资产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">的</SPAN>公</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">允价值为<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">基</SPAN>础计量<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt">，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">但</SPAN>有确凿<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">证</SPAN>据表明<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">换</SPAN>入资产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">的公</SPAN>允价值更<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">加</SPAN>可靠的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">除</SPAN>外<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt">，</SPAN>即换<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">出</SPAN>资产的</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">公允价值<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">不</SPAN>能够可<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">靠</SPAN>计量<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -4.85pt">，</SPAN>或换<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">入</SPAN>资产和<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">换</SPAN>出资产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">的</SPAN>公允价值<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">均</SPAN>能够可<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">靠</SPAN>计量但<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">有</SPAN>确凿证据</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">表明换入<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产的公<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">允</SPAN>价值更<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">加</SPAN>可靠的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">，</SPAN>应当换<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">入</SPAN>资<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">产</SPAN>的公允价<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">值</SPAN>为基础<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">计</SPAN>量。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 10.5pt 6pt 5.95pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">对于非货<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">币</SPAN>资产交<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">换</SPAN>中换入<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产和换<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">出</SPAN>资产的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">公</SPAN>允<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">价</SPAN>值均能够<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">可</SPAN>靠计量<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">的</SPAN>情形<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -4.85pt">，</SPAN>企业在</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">判断是否<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">有</SPAN>确凿证<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">据</SPAN>表明换<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">入</SPAN>资产的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">公</SPAN>允价值<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">更</SPAN>加<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">可</SPAN>靠时<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -4.8pt">，</SPAN>应当考<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">虑</SPAN>确定公<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">允</SPAN>价值所<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">使</SPAN>用的</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">输入值层次<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">企</SPAN>业可以<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">参</SPAN>考以下<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">情</SPAN>况<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">：</SPAN>第一层<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">次</SPAN>输<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">入</SPAN>值为公允<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">价</SPAN>值提供<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">了</SPAN>最可靠<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">的</SPAN>证据<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">，</SPAN>第</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">二</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">层<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt">次</SPAN>直接<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt">或</SPAN>间接<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt">可</SPAN>观<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt">察</SPAN>的输<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt">入</SPAN>值比<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt">第</SPAN>三<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt">层</SPAN>次不<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt">可</SPAN>观<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt">察</SPAN>输<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt">入</SPAN>值为<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt">公</SPAN>允价<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt">值</SPAN>提<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt">供</SPAN>更确<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt">凿</SPAN>的证</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">据<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt">。</SPAN>对于换<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">入</SPAN>资产和<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">换</SPAN>出资产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">的</SPAN>公允价<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">值</SPAN>所使用<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">的输</SPAN>入值层次<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">相</SPAN>同的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt">，</SPAN>企<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">业</SPAN>应当以<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">换</SPAN>出资产</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">的公允价<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">值</SPAN>为基础<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">计</SPAN>量<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">。</SPAN>实务中<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">，</SPAN>在<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">考</SPAN>虑了补<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">价</SPAN>因<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">素</SPAN>的调整后<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">，</SPAN>正<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">常</SPAN>交易中<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">换</SPAN>入资产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">的</SPAN>公允</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">价值和换<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">出</SPAN>资产的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">公</SPAN>允价值<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">通</SPAN>常是一<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">致</SPAN>的。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（一）会计处理原则<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 3.35pt 10.75pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">根据本准<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">则</SPAN>的规定<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt">，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">以</SPAN>公允价<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">值</SPAN>为基础<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">计</SPAN>量的非<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">货币</SPAN>性资产交<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">换</SPAN>中<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt">，</SPAN>换入<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产和换<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">出</SPAN>资</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">产的计量<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">分</SPAN>别按下<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">列</SPAN>原则进<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">行</SPAN>会计处<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">理</SPAN>：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 1.4pt 10.5pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1.</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">对于换入<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.2pt">，</SPAN>应当<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">以</SPAN>换出资<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">产</SPAN>的公允<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">价</SPAN>值和应<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">支</SPAN>付的相关<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">税</SPAN>费作为<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">换</SPAN>入资产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">的</SPAN>成本</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">进行初始<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">计</SPAN>量<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt">。</SPAN>换出<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产的公<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">允</SPAN>价值不<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">能</SPAN>够可靠<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">计量</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt">，</SPAN>或换入资<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">产</SPAN>和换出<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产的公<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">允</SPAN>价值均</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">能够可靠<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">计</SPAN>量但有<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">确</SPAN>凿证据<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">表</SPAN>明换入<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产的公<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">允</SPAN>价<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">值</SPAN>更加可靠的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -4.8pt">，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">应</SPAN>当以换<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">入</SPAN>资产的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">公</SPAN>允价</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">值和应支<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">付</SPAN>的相关<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">税</SPAN>费作为<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">换</SPAN>入资产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">的</SPAN>初始计<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">量</SPAN>金<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">额</SPAN>。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 1.8pt 10.5pt 6pt 5.95pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">其中<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -4.85pt">，</SPAN>计入换<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">入</SPAN>资产的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">应</SPAN>支付的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">相</SPAN>关税费<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">应</SPAN>当符合<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">相</SPAN>关会计准<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">则</SPAN>对资产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">初</SPAN>始计量<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">成</SPAN>本的</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">规定<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.25pt">。</SPAN>例如<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.45pt">，</SPAN>换入资<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">产</SPAN>为存货<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">的</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.25pt">，</SPAN>包括<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">相</SPAN>关税费<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.25pt">、</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">使</SPAN>该资产达<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">到</SPAN>目前场<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">所</SPAN>和状态<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">所</SPAN>发生的运</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">输费<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.25pt">、</SPAN>装卸<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">费</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.2pt">、</SPAN>保险<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">费</SPAN>以及可<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">归</SPAN>属于该<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产的其<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">他成</SPAN>本<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.25pt">；</SPAN>换入资<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">产</SPAN>为长期<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">股</SPAN>权投资<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">的</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.25pt">，</SPAN>包括</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">与取得该<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产直接<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">相</SPAN>关的费用<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">、</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">税</SPAN>金和其<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">他</SPAN>必要支<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">出</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">；</SPAN>换入资产为<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">投</SPAN>资性房<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">地</SPAN>产的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">，</SPAN>包括相</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">关税费和<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">可</SPAN>直接归<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">属</SPAN>于该资<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">产</SPAN>的其他<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">支</SPAN>出<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">；</SPAN>换入资<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">产</SPAN>为固定资<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">产</SPAN>的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">，</SPAN>包括相<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">关</SPAN>税费<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">、</SPAN>使该资</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">产达到预<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">定</SPAN>可使用<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">状</SPAN>态前所<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">发</SPAN>生的可<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">归</SPAN>属于该<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">的</SPAN>运输费<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt">、</SPAN>装<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">卸</SPAN>费<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt">、</SPAN>安装<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">费</SPAN>和专业<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">人</SPAN>员服</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">务费等<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.25pt">；</SPAN>换<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">入</SPAN>资产为<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">生</SPAN>产性生<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">物</SPAN>资产的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.45pt">，</SPAN>包括相<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">关税</SPAN>费<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.25pt">、</SPAN>运输费<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.45pt">、</SPAN>保险费<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">以</SPAN>及可直<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">接</SPAN>归属于</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">该资产的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">其</SPAN>他支出<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt">；</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">换</SPAN>入资产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">为</SPAN>无形资<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">产</SPAN>的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt">，</SPAN>包括<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">相</SPAN>关税费以<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">及</SPAN>直接归<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">属</SPAN>于使该<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产达到预</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">定用途所<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">发</SPAN>生的其<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">他</SPAN>支出。<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">上</SPAN>述税费<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">均</SPAN>不包括<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">准</SPAN>予<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">从</SPAN>增值税销<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">项</SPAN>税额中<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">抵</SPAN>扣的进<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">项</SPAN>税额。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 1.6pt 10.5pt 6pt 5.95pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2.</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">对于换出<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.25pt">，</SPAN>应当在<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">终</SPAN>止确认<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">时</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1pt">，</SPAN>将<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">换</SPAN>出资产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">的</SPAN>公允价值<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">与</SPAN>其账面<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">价</SPAN>值之间<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">的</SPAN>差额</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">计入当期<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">损</SPAN>益<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt">。</SPAN>换出<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产的公<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">允</SPAN>价值不<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">能</SPAN>够可靠<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">计量</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt">，</SPAN>或换入资<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">产</SPAN>和换出<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产的公<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">允</SPAN>价值均</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">能够可靠<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">计</SPAN>量但有<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">确</SPAN>凿证据<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">表</SPAN>明换入<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产的公<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">允</SPAN>价<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">值</SPAN>更加可靠的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.65pt">，</SPAN>应当在<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">终</SPAN>止确认时<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.65pt">，</SPAN>将换</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">入资产的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">公</SPAN>允价值<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">与</SPAN>换出资<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">产</SPAN>账面价<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">值</SPAN>之间的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">差</SPAN>额<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">计</SPAN>入当期损<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">益</SPAN>。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 1.8pt 10.5pt 6pt 5.95pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">其中，计入当期损益的会计处理视换出资产类别的不同而有所区别：（</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>1</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">）换出资产为固定资产、在建工程、生产性生物资产和无形资产的，计入当期损益的部分通过</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>“</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">资产处置</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">损益</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>”</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">科目核算，在利润表</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>“</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">资产处置收益</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>”</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">项目中列示；（</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>2</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">）换出资产为投资性房地产</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">的，按换出资产公允价值或换入资产公允价值确认其他业务收入，按换出资产账面价值结转</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">其他业务成本，二者之间的差额计入当期损益，二者分别在利润表</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>“</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">营业收入</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>”</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">和</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>“</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">营业成</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">本</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>”</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">中列示；（</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>3</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">）换出资产为长期股权投资的，计入当期损益的部分通过</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>“</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">投资收益</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>”</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">科</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">目核算，在利润表</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>“</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">投资收益</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>”</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">项目中列示。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 1.8pt 10.5pt 6pt 5.95pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">【例</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>1</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">】甲公司和乙家具制造公司均为增值税一般纳税人，适用的增值税税率均为</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>13%</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">。</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">经协商，甲公司与乙公司于</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>2×20</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">年</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>1</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">月</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>30</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">日签订资产交换合同，当日生效。合同约定，甲公</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">司以生产经营过程中使用的一台设备与乙公司生产的一批办公家具进行交换，用于交换的设备和办公家具当日的公允价值均为</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>7.5</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">万元。合同签订日即交换日，甲公司设备的账面价值为</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>7.4</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">万元（其中账面原价为</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>10</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">万元，已计提折旧</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>2.6</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">万元）；乙公司办公家具的账面价值为</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> <SPAN lang=EN-US>7</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">万元。甲公司将换入的办公家具作为固定资产使用和管理；乙公司将换入的设备作为固定资产使用和管理。甲公司和乙公司开具的增值税专用发票注明的计税价格均为</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>7.5</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">万元，增值税额</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>9,750</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">元。交易过程中，甲公司以银行存款支付设备清理费用</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>1,500</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">元。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri> <o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText
