style="MARGIN: 1.8pt 10.5pt 6pt 5.95pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">假设甲公司和乙公司此前均未对上述资产计提减值准备。整个交易过程中未发生除增值</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">税以外的其他税费。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri> <o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 1.8pt 10.5pt 6pt 5.95pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">分析：本例中，对甲公司来说，整个资产交换过程没有涉及收付货币性资产，交换的资</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">产为办公家具和设备，属于非货币性资产交换。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri> <o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 1.8pt 10.5pt 6pt 5.95pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">对甲公司来说，换入的办公家具虽然也作为固定资产使用和管理，但其未来现金流量是</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">通过员工的使用来实现，而换出的设备的未来现金流量是通过生产产品并对外销售而产生，二者产生的现金流量在风险、时间和金额方面存在明显差异，因而交换具有商业实质。同时，两项资产的公允价值都能够可靠地计量，符合以公允价值为基础计量的条件。假设没有确凿证据表明换入资产的公允价值更加可靠，按照本准则的规定，甲公司以换出资产的公允价值为基础确定换入资产的成本，并确认换出资产产生的损益。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri> <o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt 27.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">甲公司的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">账</SPAN>务处理<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">如</SPAN>下<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">：</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体"><FONT face=Calibri> 
<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 4.4pt 106pt 6pt 47.95pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: -20.9pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">借：固定<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产清理</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: 4pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;</SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体">85,25<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">0</SPAN> <o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 4.4pt 106pt 6pt 10.5pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 42pt; mso-char-indent-count: 4.0; mso-para-margin-top: 4.4pt; mso-para-margin-right: 106.0pt; mso-para-margin-bottom: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-left: 1.0gd"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">累计折旧</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri><SPAN lang=EN-US><SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN><SPAN

style='FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: "Malgun Gothic"'>的公允价</SPAN><SPAN

lang=EN-US><SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US style="mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体">6,<SPAN

<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 1.4pt 168.6pt 6pt 10.5pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 42pt; mso-char-indent-count: 4.0; mso-para-margin-top: 1.4pt; mso-para-margin-right: 168.6pt; mso-para-margin-bottom: 6.0pt; mso-para-margin-left: 1.0gd"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">资产处置<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">损</SPAN>益</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: 4.75pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;</SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体">300,<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">0</SPAN>0<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">0</SPAN> <o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 1.4pt 168.6pt 6pt 47.95pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: -20.9pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">贷：无形<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体"><FONT face=Calibri>——</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">专</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">利权</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri><SPAN lang=EN-US><SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: 5pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp;</SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体">8,<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">0</SPAN>00,00<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">0</SPAN> <o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（二）涉及补价的情形<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 3.1pt 15.5pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">根据本准<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">则</SPAN>的规定<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">，</SPAN>对<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">于</SPAN>以公允<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">价</SPAN>值为基<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">础</SPAN>计量的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">非</SPAN>货币性资<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">产</SPAN>交换<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">，</SPAN>涉及<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">补</SPAN>价的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">，</SPAN>应</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">当分别下<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">列</SPAN>情况进<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">行</SPAN>处理：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 1.65pt 15.5pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1.</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">支付补价方：（</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">）以<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt">换</SPAN>出资产的公允价值为<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt">基础</SPAN>计量的，应当以换出资产的公允价</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">值<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">，</SPAN>加上支付<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">补</SPAN>价的公<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">允</SPAN>价值和<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">应</SPAN>支付的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">相</SPAN>关税费<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.95pt">，</SPAN>作为换入<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产的成本<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">换</SPAN>出资产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">的</SPAN>公允</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">价值与其账面<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">价</SPAN>值之间的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">差</SPAN>额计入当<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">期</SPAN>损益。（</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">有确凿证据表<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">明</SPAN>换入资产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">的</SPAN>公允价值更</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">加可靠的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt">，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">即</SPAN>以换入<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产的公<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">允</SPAN>价值为<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">基</SPAN>础计量的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.65pt">，</SPAN>应当以换<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">入</SPAN>资产的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">公</SPAN>允价值<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">和</SPAN>应支付的</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">相关税费<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">作</SPAN>为换入<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产的初<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">始</SPAN>计量金额<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.65pt">，</SPAN>换入资<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">产的</SPAN>公允价值<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">减</SPAN>去支付<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">补</SPAN>价的公<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">允</SPAN>价值<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt">，</SPAN>与</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">换出资产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">账</SPAN>面价值<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">之</SPAN>间的差<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">额</SPAN>计入当<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">期</SPAN>损益。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 1.65pt 15.5pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2.</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体">收到补价方：（</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体">）以换出资产的公允价值为基础计量的，应当以换出资产的公允价值，减去收到补价的公允价值，加上应支付的相关税费，作为换入资产的成本，换出资产的公允价值与其账面价值之间的差额计入当期损益。（</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体">）有确凿证据表明换入资产的公允价值更加可靠的，即以换入资产的公允价值为基础计量的，应当以换入资产的公允价值和应支付的相关税费作为换入资产的初始计量金额，换入资产的公允价值加上收到补价的公允价值，与换出资产账面价值之间的差额计入当期损益。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 1.65pt 15.5pt 6pt 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体">【例</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体">】沿用【例</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体">】，假设其他条件不变，合同约定甲公司用于交换的设备的公允价值</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'> 
</SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体">为</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>7.5</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体">万元，乙公司用于交换的办公家具的公允价值为</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>9</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体">万元，甲公司以银行存款向乙公司支</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'> 
</SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体">付补价</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1.5</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体">万元。甲公司开具的增值税专用发票注明的计税价格</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>7.5</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体">万元，增值税额</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>9,750</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体">元；</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体">乙公司开具的增值税专用发票注明的计税价格</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>9</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体">万元，增值税额</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1.17</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体">万元；甲公司以银行存</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体">款向乙公司支付增值税差额</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1,950</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体">元。</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'> 
<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 1.65pt 15.5pt 6pt 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体">分析：本例中，涉及收付货币性资产，应当计算货币性资产占整个资产交换的比例。对</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体">于甲公司，支付的货币性资产</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1.5</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体">万元占换入资产公允价值</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>9</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体">万元（或换出资产公允价值</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>7.5 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体">万元和支付的货币性资产</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1.5</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体">万元之和）的比例为</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>16.67&lt;25%</SPAN><SPAN

lang=EN-US

<P class=MsoBodyText

</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">资产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt">，</SPAN>或同<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">时</SPAN>以多项<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">非</SPAN>货币性<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产换入<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">另</SPAN>一企业<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">的一</SPAN>项非货币<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">性</SPAN>资产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt">，</SPAN>或<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">以</SPAN>多项非<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">货</SPAN>币性资</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">产同时换<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">入</SPAN>另一企<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">业</SPAN>的多项<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">非</SPAN>货币性<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt">，</SPAN>这些<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">交换</SPAN>也可能涉<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">及</SPAN>补价<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt">。</SPAN>对<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">于</SPAN>涉及换<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">入</SPAN>或换出</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">多项资产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">的</SPAN>非货币<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">性</SPAN>资产交<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">换</SPAN>的计量<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -4.85pt">，</SPAN>企<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">业</SPAN>同样应<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">当</SPAN>首先判断<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">是</SPAN>否符合<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">本</SPAN>准则以<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">公</SPAN>允价值为</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">基础计量<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">的</SPAN>两个条件<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.65pt">，</SPAN>再按本<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">准</SPAN>则的规<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">定</SPAN>分别情<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">况确</SPAN>定各项换<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">入</SPAN>资产的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">初</SPAN>始计量<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">金</SPAN>额<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt">，</SPAN>以及</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">各项换出<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产终止<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">确</SPAN>认的相<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">关</SPAN>损益。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 5.25pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">涉及换入多项<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产或换出<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">多</SPAN>项资产的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">非</SPAN>货币性资产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">交</SPAN>换符合以公允<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">价</SPAN>值为基础<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">计</SPAN>量的，</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">通常可以<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">分</SPAN>为以下<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">情</SPAN>形：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 1.25pt 0cm 6pt 27.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><FONT size=3><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1.</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">以换出资<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">产</SPAN>的公<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">允</SPAN>价值为<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">基</SPAN>础计量<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">的</SPAN>。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 3.6pt 0cm 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">（</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">）对于同时<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">换</SPAN>入的多项<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产，由于<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">通</SPAN>常无法将<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">换</SPAN>入资产与换出<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">的</SPAN>某项特定<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产相对</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">应<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -5.05pt">，</SPAN>应当按<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">照</SPAN>各项换<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">入</SPAN>资产的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">公</SPAN>允价值<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">的</SPAN>相对比<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -5.05pt">例</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">（换</SPAN>入资产的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">公</SPAN>允价值<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">不</SPAN>能够可<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">靠</SPAN>计量的，</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">可以按照<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">各</SPAN>项换入<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产的原<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">账</SPAN>面价值<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">的</SPAN>相对比<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">例</SPAN>或<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">其</SPAN>他合理的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">比</SPAN>例<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt">），</SPAN>将换<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">出</SPAN>资产公<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">允</SPAN>价值</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">总<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">额</SPAN>（涉及补<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">价</SPAN>的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">，</SPAN>加上支<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">付</SPAN>补价的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">公</SPAN>允价值<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">或</SPAN>减<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">去</SPAN>收到补价<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">的</SPAN>公允价值<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">分</SPAN>摊至各<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">项</SPAN>换入</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">资产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -5.05pt">，</SPAN>以分<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">摊</SPAN>额和应<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">支</SPAN>付的相<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">关</SPAN>税费作<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">为</SPAN>各项换<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">入资</SPAN>产的成本<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">进</SPAN>行初始<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">计</SPAN>量<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -5.05pt">。</SPAN>需要<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">说</SPAN>明的是，</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">根据本准<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">则</SPAN>规定<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt">，</SPAN>如<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">果</SPAN>同时换<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">入</SPAN>的多项<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">非</SPAN>货币性<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资产</SPAN>中包含<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt">由</SPAN>《<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">企</SPAN>业会计<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">准</SPAN>则第</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>22</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">号</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US style="mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
face=Calibri>——</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">金</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">融工具确<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">认</SPAN>和计量<SPAN

style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产<SPAN

style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">照</SPAN>《<SPAN

style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>22</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">号</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体">—</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US style="mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体">—</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">金融<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">工</SPAN>具确认和</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">计量<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">》</SPAN>的规定<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">进</SPAN>行会计<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">处</SPAN>理<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">，</SPAN>在确定<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">换</SPAN>入的其<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">他</SPAN>多<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">项</SPAN>资产的初<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">始</SPAN>计量金<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">额</SPAN>时<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">，</SPAN>应当将<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">金</SPAN>融资</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">产公允价<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">值</SPAN>从换出<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产公允<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">价</SPAN>值总额<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">中</SPAN>扣除。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 1.6pt 0cm 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">（</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">）对于同时<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">换</SPAN>出的多项<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产，应当<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">将</SPAN>各项换出<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产的公允价值<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">与</SPAN>其账面价<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">值</SPAN>之间的</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">差额，在<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">各</SPAN>项换出<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产终止<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">确</SPAN>认时计<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">入</SPAN>当期损<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">益</SPAN>。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 1.9pt 0cm 6pt 27.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><FONT size=3><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2.</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">以换入资<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">产</SPAN>的公<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">允</SPAN>价值为<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">基</SPAN>础计量<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">的。</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 3.6pt 0cm 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">（</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">）对于同时<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">换</SPAN>入的多项<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产，应当<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">以</SPAN>各项换入<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产的公允价值<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">和</SPAN>应支付的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">相</SPAN>关税费</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">作为各项<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">换</SPAN>入资产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">的</SPAN>初始计<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">量</SPAN>金额。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 1.6pt 0cm 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">（</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">2</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">）对于同时换出的多项资产，由于通常无法将换入资产与换出的某项特定资产相对</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">应，应当按照各项换出资产的公允价值的相对比例（换出资产的公允价值不能够可靠计量的，</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">可以按照各项换出资产的账面价值的相对比例），将换入资产的公允价值总额（涉及补价的，</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">减去支付补价的公允价值或加上收到补价的公允价值）分摊至各项换出资产，分摊额与各项换出资产账面价值之间的差额，在各项换出资产终止确认时计入当期损益。需要说明的是，</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">根据本准则规定，如果同时换出的多项非货币性资产中包含由《企业会计准则第</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">22</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">号</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>——</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">金</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">融工具确认和计量》规范的金融资产，该金融资产应当按照《企业会计准则第</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">22</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">号</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>——</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">金融</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">工具确认和计量》和《企业会计准则第</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">23</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">号</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>——</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">金融资产转移》的规定判断换出的该金融资</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">产是否满足终止确认条件并进行终止确认的会计处理，在确定其他各项换出资产终止确认的</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">相关损益时，应当将终止确认的金融资产公允价值从换入资产公允价值总额中扣除。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 1.6pt 0cm 6pt 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt" 
align=left><FONT size=3><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体">【例<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>5</SPAN>】</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">甲公司和乙公司均为增值税一般纳税人。经协商，甲公司和乙公司于</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>2×20</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">年</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>1 </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">月</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>25</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">日签订资产交换合同，当日生效。合同约定，甲公司用于交换的资产包括：一间生产用</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">厂房，公允价值为</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>110</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">万元；一幢自购入时就全部用于经营出租的公寓楼，公允价值为</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>390 </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">万元。乙公司用于交换的资产包括：一块土地的使用权，公允价值为</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>240</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">万元；经营过程中</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">使用的</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>10</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">辆货车，公允价值为</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>300</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">万元。甲公司以银行存款向乙公司支付补价</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>40</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">万元。双方</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">于</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>2×20</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">年</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>2</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">月</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>1</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">日完成了资产交换手续。交换当日，甲公司的厂房的账面价值为</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>120</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">万元（其中账面原价为</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>150</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">万元，已计提折旧</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>30</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">万元），作为采用成本模式计量的投资性房地产的公寓楼的账面价值为</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>360</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">万元（其中账面原价为</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>420</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">万元，已计提折旧</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>60</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">万元），乙公司的土地</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">使用权的账面价值为</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>210</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">万元（其中成本</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>220</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">万元，累计摊销额为</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>10</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">万元），</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>10</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">辆货车的账面</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">价值为</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>320</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">万元（其中账面原价为</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>400</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">万元，已计提折旧</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>80</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">万元）。甲公司开具两张增值税专</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">用发票，分别注明厂房的计税价格</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>110</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">万元、增值税额</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>9.9</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">万元；公寓楼的计税价格</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>390</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">万元、</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">增值税额</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>35.1</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">万元。乙公司开具两张增值税专用发票，分别注明土地使用权的计税价格</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>240 </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">万元、增值税额</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>21.6</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">万元；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>10</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">辆货车的计税价格</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>300</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">万元、增值税额</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>39</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">万元。甲公司以银行</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">存款向乙公司支付增值税差额</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>15.6</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">万元。交易过程中，甲公司用银行存款支付了土地使用权</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">的契税及过户费用</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>5</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">万元，乙公司用银行存款分别支付了厂房和公寓楼的契税及过户费用</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>3 </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">万元和</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>10</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">万元。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri> <o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 1.6pt 0cm 6pt 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt" 
align=left><FONT size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">假设甲公司和乙公司此前均未对上述资产计提减值准备，上述资产交换后的用途不发生</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">改变。不考虑其他税费。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri> <o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 1.6pt 0cm 6pt 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt" 
align=left><FONT size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">分析：本例中，涉及收付货币性资产，应当计算货币性资产占整个资产交换的比例。补</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">价</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>40</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">万元占整个资产交换金额</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>540</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">万元的比例为</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>7.41%&lt;25%</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">，属于非货币性资产交换。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri> <o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 1.6pt 0cm 6pt 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt" 
align=left><FONT size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">本例中用于交换的厂房是通过在厂房使用寿命内与其他资产协同生产产品并对外销售</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">而产生现金流量，公寓楼是通过经营出租并定期收取租金而产生稳定均衡的现金流量，土地</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">使用权是通过在其上建造房屋后与房屋共同产生现金流量，货车是通过使用或提供服务而产</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">生独立的现金流量，各项资产的未来现金流量在风险、时间和金额方面均明显不同，因而交</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">换具有商业实质。同时，各项资产的公允价值都能够可靠地计量，符合以公允价值为基础计</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">量的条件。假设均没有确凿证据表明换入资产的公允价值更加可靠，甲公司和乙公司均以换</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">出资产的公允价值为基础确定各项换入资产的成本，并确认各项换出资产产生的损益。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri> <o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 1.6pt 0cm 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">甲公司的会计处理如下：</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> <SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 1.6pt 0cm 6pt 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">（</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US style="mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
face=Calibri>1</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">）确定<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">各</SPAN>项换入<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产的初<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">始</SPAN>计量金<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">额。</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体"><FONT face=Calibri> 
<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0.3pt 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US style="FONT-SIZE: 2pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p><FONT 
face=Calibri>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>

    <TD

</SPAN><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: 4pt"><SPAN

<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt 32.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><FONT size=3><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Malgun Gothic",sans-serif; mso-bidi-font-family: "Malgun Gothic"'>【例</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Arial",sans-serif; mso-fareast-font-family: Arial'>6</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Malgun Gothic",sans-serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt; mso-bidi-font-family: "Malgun Gothic"'>】</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">沿<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.25pt">用</SPAN>【例</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体"><FONT face=Calibri>5</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LETTER-SPACING: -1pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">】，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">假</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">设其<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">他</SPAN>条件不变<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.25pt">，</SPAN>合同约<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">定</SPAN>甲公司用<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">于</SPAN>交换的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产还包<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">括</SPAN>一项</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 3.6pt 10.6pt 6pt 10.9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><FONT size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">对</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US style="mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
face=Calibri>P</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">公司的股票<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">投</SPAN>资，甲公<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">司</SPAN>将该投资<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">作</SPAN>为交易性<SPAN

lang=EN-US style="mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
face=Calibri>1</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">月</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> <SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体">25</SPAN></FONT><SPAN

style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">0</SPAN></FONT></SPAN><SPAN

style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">，</SPAN>账面<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">价</SPAN>值为</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体"><FONT face=Calibri>25</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">万</SPAN><SPAN

<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 1.65pt 10.6pt 6pt 10.9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt"><FONT

style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">，</SPAN>沿用【例</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US

style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">】</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">的分析，<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">甲</SPAN>公司和乙<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">公</SPAN>司均以换出资<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">产</SPAN>的公允价<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">值</SPAN>为基础确定各项<SPAN

style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">的</SPAN>成本<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">，</SPAN>并确<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">认</SPAN>各项换<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">出</SPAN>资产产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">生</SPAN>的损益<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">。</SPAN>另外<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">，</SPAN>甲<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">公</SPAN>司和乙<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">公</SPAN>司用于交换的非货<SPAN

style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">中</SPAN>包含交<SPAN

style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt">，</SPAN>属于<SPAN

style="mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体"><FONT face=Calibri>22</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">号</SPAN><SPAN

      style="TEXT-ALIGN: right; MARGIN: 4.25pt 5.2pt 0pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%" 
      align=right><SPAN lang=EN-US 
      style='FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>0<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P></TD>
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 16.55pt; BORDER-RIGHT: black 1pt solid; WIDTH: 55.2pt; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 0cm; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 0cm; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-height-rule: exactly; mso-border-alt: solid black .75pt; mso-border-left-alt: solid black .75pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid black .75pt"

      style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">,</SPAN>000<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P></TD></TR></TBODY></TABLE></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 2pt 92.85pt 6pt 32.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><FONT size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">（</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US style="mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
face=Calibri>2</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">）确定<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">各</SPAN>项换出<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产终止<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">确</SPAN>认的相<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">关</SPAN>损益<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">。</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体"><FONT face=Calibri> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">同【例</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US style="mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
face=Calibri>5</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">】<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">，</SPAN>此处略<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">。</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体"><FONT face=Calibri> 
<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 1.65pt 0cm 6pt 32.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><FONT size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">（</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US style="mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
face=Calibri>3</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">）乙公<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">司</SPAN>的账务<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">处</SPAN>理：略<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">。</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体"><FONT face=Calibri> 
<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0.15pt 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US style="FONT-SIZE: 5pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><o:p><FONT 
face=Calibri>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><A name=七、关于以账面价值为基础计量></A><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>七、关于以账面价值为基础计量<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 3.8pt 10.5pt 6pt 11pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">根据本准<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">则</SPAN>的规定<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -4.85pt">，</SPAN>当<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">非</SPAN>货币性<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产交换<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">不</SPAN>满足本<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">准</SPAN>则规定的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">以</SPAN>公允价<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">值</SPAN>为基础<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">计</SPAN>量的</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">条件时<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt">，</SPAN>即<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">非</SPAN>货币性<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产交换<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">不</SPAN>具有商<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">业</SPAN>实质<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt">，</SPAN>或<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">者</SPAN>虽然具有<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">商</SPAN>业实质<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">但</SPAN>换入资<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">产</SPAN>和换出资</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">产的公允<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">价</SPAN>值均不<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">能</SPAN>可靠计<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">量</SPAN>的，企<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">业</SPAN>应当以<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">账</SPAN>面<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">价</SPAN>值为基础<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">计</SPAN>量。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><A name=（一）会计处理原则></A><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（一）会计处理原则<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 3.35pt 0cm 6pt 11pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1.</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">对于换入<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.2pt">，</SPAN>应当<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">以</SPAN>换出资<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">产</SPAN>的账面<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">价</SPAN>值和应<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">支</SPAN>付的相关<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">税</SPAN>费作为<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">换</SPAN>入资产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">的</SPAN>初始</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">计量金额。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 2.05pt 0cm 6pt 32.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><FONT size=3><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2.</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">对于换出<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产，<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">终</SPAN>止确认<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">时</SPAN>不确认<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">损</SPAN>益。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 2.35pt 0cm 6pt 11pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Malgun Gothic",sans-serif; mso-bidi-font-family: "Malgun Gothic"'>【例</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Arial",sans-serif; mso-fareast-font-family: Arial'>7</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Malgun Gothic",sans-serif; mso-bidi-font-family: "Malgun Gothic"'>】</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">甲公司<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">是</SPAN>一家制药<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">公</SPAN>司，因经<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">营</SPAN>战略发生<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">重</SPAN>大转变，将专<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">注</SPAN>于疫苗的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">生</SPAN>产和销</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">售，其拥有的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">一</SPAN>项生产抗<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">生</SPAN>素的专利<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">权</SPAN>难以满足<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">新的</SPAN>经营战略。乙<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">公</SPAN>司也是一<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">家</SPAN>制药公司，</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">正在开展<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">一</SPAN>系列抗<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">生</SPAN>素方面<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">的</SPAN>新业务<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">。</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体"><FONT face=Calibri>2×<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">2</SPAN>0</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">年</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US style="mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
face=Calibri>3</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">月</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US style="mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体"><FONT face=Calibri>3<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">0</SPAN></FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">日<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">，</SPAN>甲公司和<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">乙</SPAN>公司协<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">商</SPAN>后决定<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">，</SPAN>甲公</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">司将其抗<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">生</SPAN>素的专<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">利</SPAN>权转让<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">给</SPAN>乙公司<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt">，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">作</SPAN>为交换<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt">，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">乙</SPAN>公司将其<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">刚</SPAN>申请专<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">利</SPAN>的一项<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">传</SPAN>染病疫苗</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">配方转让<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">给</SPAN>甲公司<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">，</SPAN>由<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">其</SPAN>进行生<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">产</SPAN>推广<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">。</SPAN>当日<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">，</SPAN>甲<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">公</SPAN>司换出的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">抗</SPAN>生素专<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">利</SPAN>权的账<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">面</SPAN>价值为</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体"><FONT face=Calibri>45 </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">万<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.25pt">元</SPAN>（其中<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">账</SPAN>面原价<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">为</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体"><FONT face=Calibri>60</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">万元<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.45pt">，</SPAN>累计摊<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">销</SPAN>额为</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体"><FONT face=Calibri>15</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">万元</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LETTER-SPACING: -1.25pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">）；</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">乙公司<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">刚</SPAN>申请专<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">利</SPAN>的传染<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">病</SPAN>疫苗已</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">转为无形<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产核算<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">，</SPAN>账<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">面</SPAN>价值为</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体"><FONT face=Calibri>5<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">0</SPAN></FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">万元<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">，</SPAN>尚未<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">进</SPAN>行<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">摊</SPAN>销<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">。</SPAN>假设两项<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">专</SPAN>利权的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">公</SPAN>允价值<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">不</SPAN>能可</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">靠计量<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">。</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体"><FONT face=Calibri> 
<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText

align=left><FONT size=3><SPAN
