<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><A name=（二）涉及补价的情形></A><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（二）涉及补价的情形<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 3.35pt 0cm 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">根据本准<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">则</SPAN>的规定<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">，</SPAN>对<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">于</SPAN>以账面<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">价</SPAN>值为基<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">础</SPAN>计量的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">非</SPAN>货币性资<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">产</SPAN>交换<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">，</SPAN>涉及<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">补</SPAN>价的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">，</SPAN>应当将补价<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">作</SPAN>为确定<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">换</SPAN>入资产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">初</SPAN>始计量<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">金</SPAN>额的调<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">整</SPAN>因<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">素</SPAN>，分别下<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">列</SPAN>情况进<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">行</SPAN>处理：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 1.4pt 0cm 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1.</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">支付补价<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">方</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1pt">：</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">应</SPAN>当以换<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">出</SPAN>资产的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">账</SPAN>面价<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">值</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1pt">，</SPAN>加上<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">支</SPAN>付补价的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">账</SPAN>面价值<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">和</SPAN>应支付<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">的</SPAN>相关税费，作<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">为</SPAN>换入资<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">产</SPAN>的初始<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">计</SPAN>量金额<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">，</SPAN>不确认<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">损</SPAN>益。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 1.9pt 0cm 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2.</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">收到补价<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">方</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.75pt">：</SPAN>应当<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">以</SPAN>换出资<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">产</SPAN>的账面<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">价</SPAN>值<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.75pt">，</SPAN>减<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">去收</SPAN>到补价的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">公</SPAN>允价值<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.75pt">，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">加</SPAN>上应支<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">付</SPAN>的相关税费<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">，</SPAN>作为换<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">入</SPAN>资产的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">初</SPAN>始计量<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">金</SPAN>额，不<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">确</SPAN>认<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">损</SPAN>益。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><A 
name=（三）涉及换入多项资产或换出多项资产的情形></A><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>（三）涉及换入多项资产或换出多项资产的情形<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 1.4pt 0cm 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体">对于以账面价值为基础计量的非货币性资产交换，如涉及换入多项资产或换出多项资产，</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体">或者同时换入和换出多项资产的，应当分别对换入的多项资产、换出的多项资产进行会计处理。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 1.4pt 0cm 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt" 
align=left><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1.</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体">对于换入的多项资产，由于通常无法将换出资产与换入的某项特定资产相对应，应当</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体">按照各项换入资产的公允价值的相对比例（换入资产的公允价值不能够可靠计量的，也可以</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体">按照各项换入资产的原账面价值的相对比例或其他合理的比例），将换出资产的账面价值总</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'> 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体">额（涉及补价的，加上支付补价的账面价值或减去收到补价的公允价值）分摊至各项换入资产，加上应支付的相关税费，作为各项换入资产的初始计量金额。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 1.4pt 0cm 6pt 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2.</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体">对于同时换出的多项资产，各项换出资产终止确认时均不确认损益。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 2.1pt 15.5pt 6pt 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Malgun Gothic",sans-serif; mso-bidi-font-family: "Malgun Gothic"'>【例</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Arial",sans-serif; mso-fareast-font-family: Arial'>8</SPAN><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Malgun Gothic",sans-serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt; mso-bidi-font-family: "Malgun Gothic"'>】</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">沿</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LETTER-SPACING: -0.75pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">用</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">【<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">例</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体"><FONT face=Calibri>7</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LETTER-SPACING: -1pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">】</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LETTER-SPACING: -0.75pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">假设<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">其</SPAN>他条件<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">不</SPAN>变<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.75pt">，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">甲</SPAN>公司<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">和</SPAN>乙公司进<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">行</SPAN>专利权<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">交</SPAN>换的同<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">时</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.75pt">，</SPAN>甲</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">公司还将<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">一</SPAN>套抗生<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">素</SPAN>生产专<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">用</SPAN>设备转<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">移</SPAN>给乙公司<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -4.85pt">，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">乙</SPAN>公司将一<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">套</SPAN>专门用<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">于</SPAN>传染病<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">疫</SPAN>苗存储的</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">设备转移给甲<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">公</SPAN>司。</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体"><FONT face=Calibri>2×20</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">年</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US style="mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
face=Calibri>3</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">月</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US style="mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
face=Calibri>30</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">日<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">，</SPAN>甲公司换出<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">的</SPAN>专用设备的账<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">面</SPAN>价值为</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体"><FONT face=Calibri>42<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">0</SPAN></FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">万元（其中</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">账面原价为</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体">5</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US style="mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体">00</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">万元<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">，</SPAN>已<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">计</SPAN>提折旧</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体">8</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US style="mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体">0</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">万元<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">），</SPAN>乙公<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">司换</SPAN>出的疫苗<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">存</SPAN>储设备<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">账</SPAN>面价值为</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体">4</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US style="mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体">00</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">万元（其中账<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">面</SPAN>原价为</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体"><FONT face=Calibri>70<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">0</SPAN></FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">万元<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">，</SPAN>已<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">计</SPAN>提折旧</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体"><FONT face=Calibri>30<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">0</SPAN></FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">万元<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">）。</SPAN>假设两项<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">设</SPAN>备均为<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">自</SPAN>行研究<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">制</SPAN>造的专用</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">设备，其<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">公</SPAN>允价值<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">不</SPAN>能可靠<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">计</SPAN>量<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">。</SPAN></SPAN><FONT face=Calibri><SPAN 
style="mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体"> </SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 1.25pt 0cm 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">分析<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -5.05pt">：</SPAN>本例中<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -5.3pt">，</SPAN>由于用<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">于</SPAN>交换的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">两</SPAN>项药物<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">专</SPAN>利和两<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">套设</SPAN>备的公允<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">价</SPAN>值均不<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">能</SPAN>可靠地<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">计</SPAN>量，</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">因此甲公<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">司</SPAN>和乙公<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">司</SPAN>均应当<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">以</SPAN>换出资<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">产</SPAN>的账面<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">价</SPAN>值<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">为</SPAN>基础确定<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">换</SPAN>入资产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">的</SPAN>初始计<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">量</SPAN>金额<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -4.85pt">，</SPAN>换出资产不确认<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">损</SPAN>益。对于<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">同</SPAN>时换入的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">多</SPAN>项资产，<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">由于</SPAN>换入资产的公<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">允</SPAN>价值不能<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">可</SPAN>靠地计量，甲公司和<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">乙</SPAN>公司均<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">按</SPAN>照各项<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">换</SPAN>入资产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">的</SPAN>原账面<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">价</SPAN>值<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">的</SPAN>相对比例<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -4.85pt">，</SPAN>将<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">换</SPAN>出资产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">的</SPAN>账面价<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">值</SPAN>总额分摊至各<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">项</SPAN>换入资产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">作</SPAN>为各项<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">换</SPAN>入资产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">的</SPAN>初始计<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">量</SPAN>金额<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">。</SPAN>对于同<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">时</SPAN>换出的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">多</SPAN>项资产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">，</SPAN>终止确认时按<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">照</SPAN>账面价<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">值</SPAN>转销，<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">不</SPAN>确认损<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">益。</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体"><FONT face=Calibri> 
<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt 27.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">甲公司的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">会</SPAN>计处理<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">如</SPAN>下<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">：</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体"><FONT face=Calibri> 
<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 4.4pt 0cm 6pt 27.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%"><FONT size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">（</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US style="mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
face=Calibri>1</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">）确定<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">各</SPAN>项换入<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产的初<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">始</SPAN>计量金<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">额。</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体"><FONT face=Calibri> 
<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText

style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">（</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US style="mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
face=Calibri>2</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">）对于<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">同</SPAN>时换出<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">的</SPAN>多项资<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">产</SPAN>，终止<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">确</SPAN>认时<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">按</SPAN>照<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">账</SPAN>面价值转<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">销</SPAN>，不确<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">认</SPAN>损益<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">。</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体"><FONT face=Calibri> 
<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>

<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><A 
name=八、关于非货币性资产交换的披露></A><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>八、关于非货币性资产交换的披露<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 4.05pt 10.5pt 6pt 11pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">本准则规定，<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">企</SPAN>业应当在<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">附</SPAN>注中披露<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">有</SPAN>关非货币性<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产交换的下列<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">信</SPAN>息：（</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">）<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">非</SPAN>货币</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">性资产交<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">换</SPAN>是否具<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">有</SPAN>商业实<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">质</SPAN>及其原因<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.45pt">；</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">（</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LETTER-SPACING: -0.75pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">换入<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">资</SPAN>产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.75pt">、</SPAN>换出资<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">产</SPAN>的类别<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.45pt">；</SPAN>（</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LETTER-SPACING: -1pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">换入资产</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">初始计量<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">金</SPAN>额的确<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">定</SPAN>方式<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -5.05pt">；</SPAN>（</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">换<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">入</SPAN>资产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.65pt">、</SPAN>换出资<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">产</SPAN>的公允价<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">值</SPAN>以及换<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">出</SPAN>资产的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">账</SPAN>面价值；（</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>5</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">）非货<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">币</SPAN>性资产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">交</SPAN>换确认<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">的</SPAN>损益。</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">需要说明的是，在披露非货币性资产交换是否具有商业实质的原因时，如果能够通过定性分析即可得出结论认定换入资产的未来现金流量在风险、时间或金额方面与换出资产显著不同，交换因而具有商业实质，则应当披露定性分析中所考虑的相关因素和相关结论。在这种情况下，不需要进一步披露使用换入资产和继续使用换出资产所产生的预计未来现金流量现值，以及通过计算进行的定量分析。如果难以通过定性分析直接得出结论认定非货币性资</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">产交换具有商业实质，则应当披露使用换入资产进行相关经营的预计未来现金流量现值和继</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">续使用换出资产进行相关经营的预计未来现金流量现值，以及相关的定量分析和结论。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P style="LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><A name=九、关于新旧准则的衔接规定></A><SPAN 
style="mso-ascii-font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: 宋体; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"><FONT 
face=宋体><FONT size=3>九、关于新旧准则的衔接规定<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 3.8pt 0cm 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21.1pt"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">本准则自</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>20<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">1</SPAN>9</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">年</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US

lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">0</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">日起施行<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.95pt">。</SPAN>本准则<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">规</SPAN>定<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">，</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2006</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">年</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN><SPAN

lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>15</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">日财<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">政</SPAN>部印发<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.7pt">的</SPAN>《<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">财</SPAN>政部关</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">于印<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.75pt">发</SPAN>〈企<SPAN

style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.75pt">〉</SPAN>等</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US

style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">货币性资<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">产</SPAN>交换》同<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">时</SPAN>废止。财政部<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">此</SPAN>前发布的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">有</SPAN>关非货币性</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> 
</FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">资产交换<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">会</SPAN>计处理<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">规</SPAN>定与本<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">准</SPAN>则不一<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">致</SPAN>的，以<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">本</SPAN>准<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">则</SPAN>为准。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText
